#include <LiquidCrystal.h>
const int rs=12,en=11,d4=5,d5=4,d6=3,d7=2;
LiquidCrystal lcd(rs,en,d4,d5,d6,d7);
void setup()
{
  lcd.begin(16,2);
  lcd.print("Hello, Atharv");
}
void loop()
{
  lcd.setCursor(0,1);
  for (int positionCounter = 0; positionCounter < 13; positionCounter++) {
    lcd.scrollDisplayLeft();
    delay(150);
  }

}

Hokay, hopefully this helps:
| Command | Param | Info |
|-|-|-|
| ~add | <trip> | Add ModBot user |
| ~remove | <trip> | Remove ModBot user |
| ~kick | <nick> | Remove user from channel |
| ~lockroom |  | Prevent users from joining this channel |
| ~unlockroom |  | Allow users to join this channel |

ELIZA can help more if you need it, google it.
RIP original ModBot. . .

| Command | Param | Info |
|-|-|-|
| ~add | <trip> | Add ModBot user |
| ~remove | <trip> | Remove ModBot user |
| ~kick | <nick> | Remove user from channel |
| ~lockroom |  | Prevent users from joining this channel |
| ~unlockroom |  | Allow users to join this channel |

ELIZA can help more if you need it, google it.
RIP original ModBot. . .
